{'Subject': 'Rep. Shawnna Bolick: Arizona Supreme Court Decision A Victory for the Flat Tax and Arizona Taxpayers', 'From': 'Shawnna Bolick <info@bolickforarizona.com>', 'Message': [<p>Rep. Shawnna Bolick: Arizona Supreme Court Decision A Victory for the Flat Tax and Arizona Taxpayers
April 21, 2022
FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE
Contact: joanna@theresolute.group

PHOENIX, Ariz. — Today, the Arizona Supreme Court rejected a referendum placing Senate Bill 1828, Sections 13 and 15 on the ballot for the 2022 General Election. This referendum was filed by Invest in Arizona (sponsored by the Arizona Education Association and Stand for Children), a political action committee funded by out-of-state left wing donors.

“This is a huge victory for Arizona taxpayers. This decision comes at a time when Biden’s inflationary economy is making Arizonans choose between filling up their gas tank or providing food for their families,” Rep. Bolick said, adding, “I am also hopeful the Arizona Legislature can further reduce the flat tax this legislative session and deliver much needed relief.”

Sections 13 and 15 of Senate Bill 1828 will impose a “flat” tax of 2.5% on taxable income, which becomes effective if General Fund revenues reach specified targets.

Shawnna Bolick is an Arizona State Representative for LD-20 and is running for Arizona Secretary of State.

{'Subject': 'AG Audit reveals depth of Maricopa County chain of custody and signature verification flaws.', 'From': 'Shawnna Bolick <info@bolickforarizona.com>', 'Message': [<p>I’m Leading the Fight for Secure Elections

Good morning Freedom Fighters,

Almost two years ago, Arizonans watched in horror as Maricopa County Recorder Adrian Fontes and Secretary of State Katie Hobbs used the pandemic as an excuse not to follow the laws and procedures, taking full advantage of the opportunity to tilt the scales in their favor. The chaos they contrived left our elections vulnerable for bad actors to manipulate their ineptitude.

The Arizona State Senate audited  the 2020 Maricopa County election and the Attorney General finally released his interim report (https://www.azag.gov/sites/default/files/2022-04/2022-04-06%20Fann%20letter.pdf?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID) on it.

I’ve been leading the fight for increased security in our elections at the legislature, and I’m taking my vision for secure elections to the Secretary of State's office. I’m not going to allow Democrats to federalize our elections - or relive the chaos of 2020 - again.
STAND UP FOR SECURE ELECTIONS (https://secure.winred.com/vote-bolick/donate?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID)
The interim report (https://www.azag.gov/sites/default/files/2022-04/2022-04-06%20Fann%20letter.pdf?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID) revealed the depth of Arizona’s serious election flaws in 2020. A few highlights:
* “The early ballot signature verification system in Maricopa County is insufficient to guard against abuse…” and “vulnerable to error, fraud, and oversight.”
* The number of early ballots rejected due to missing or mismatched signatures has been steadily declining since 2018 when Adrian Fontes became County Recorder — despite the number of overall early ballots increasing.
* “Maricopa County failed to follow the Elections Procedures Manual when transporting 20% of the early ballots.”
* “Between 100,000 and 200,000 ballots were transported without a proper chain of custody.”

It isn’t too late to secure our elections, but I NEED YOUR help.  Help me continue this fight for our election integrity.
Please volunteer for my campaign to be Arizona’s Chief Election Official (https://www.bolickforarizona.com/join-bolicks-brigade/?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID)
I built a robust Roadmap to Restore Election Integrity (https://www.bolickforarizona.com/roadmap-to-restore-election-integrity/?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID) with the input from Arizonans like you that serves as our guiding document for this fight to secure our elections. Our election laws need to be updated, but even more importantly, our laws need teeth.  That’s why I sponsored  HB 2783 (https://www.azleg.gov/legtext/55leg/2R/bills/HB2783H.pdf?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID) , which increases penalties on election officials who knowingly violate our election laws.

I also sponsored HB 2379 (https://www.azleg.gov/legtext/55leg/2R/bills/HB2379H.pdf?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID)  and HB 2378 (https://www.azleg.gov/legtext/55leg/2R/bills/HB2378H.pdf?mc_cid=6d5fa8ae29&amp;mc_eid=UNIQID) , which restricts the ability for the Secretary of State to break the law for the benefit of their party. These bills would prevent the Secretary of State from unilaterally settling election lawsuits via consent decree and establishing election procedures which ignore the rule of law. Hobbs previously used these loopholes to take over our elections in 2020, so we’re closing those gaps.

Thank you once again for your continued support,
Shawnna Bolick

{'Subject': 'Thank you! Let me introduce myself', 'From': '"Rep. Beau LaFave for SOS" <BeauLaFaveSOS@gmail.com>', 'Message': [<p>Thank you for volunteering your time to attend State Convention in Grand Rapids on April 23rd. You get to decide who we put-up against SOS Benson

View this email in your browser (https://mailchi.mp/73e2f970bf80/thank-you-let-me-introduce-myself?e=a51be6a145)
Thank you for volunteering your time to attend State Convention in Grand Rapids to decide Michigan's Republican nominee for Secretary of State!

My name is State Representative Beau LaFave, and I am going to beat incumbent Democrat Secretary of State Jocelyn Benson.

You have three choices to be the GOP nominee for Secretary of State. Any of the three of us would be better than Jocelyn Benson. But being a better option means nothing if you cannot beat Benson in November.

I ask you to consider what kind of fight you think the Dems will put up for this race. Do you think they’re mildly interested in the outcome, or do you think they will bring out the heavy artillery?

Of all three candidates, I’m the only one who ever took on the full force of the Democrat Party and walked away a winner.

Since I announced my campaign for SOS in October, I have personally:
driven 37,000 miles, cold-called 2500 delegates, and attended countless amazing Republican events from Marquette to Monroe telling my story. It proves I am the fighter and winner we need to take the Democrats on in November and deliver the Office of Secretary of State back to the Republicans

Fighting and winning against the odds

I was born and raised in Iron Mountain, MI (cross the Mighty Mac, turn left, drive 3 more hours). I was air-lifted and spent my first six weeks at Milwaukee Children’s Hospital. But, I was a fighter, and I beat the odds.

At eighteen months, my left leg was amputated. I was not given a lot of hope for walking. I beat those odds too.

I graduated from Michigan State University and entered Wayne State University Law School, but I kept my eye on my hometown happenings – particularly the politics. A very popular Democrat Sheriff  declared for State Representative in an area that ALWAYS alternates between a Democrat and Republican State Rep. It was the Dem’s turn that year.

I spent a year searching for a candidate who could beat this popular Sheriff.  I realized that person was me, a 23-year-old law student. So, I passed my finals, packed up, and went back home. After winning a primary I wasn’t supposed to (beat those odds too!), I suddenly found myself one-on-one against that very popular Sheriff. The Sheriff  had LOTS of help. The Dems needed that seat to take majority. So they spent $600,000 in the cheapest media market this side of the Mississippi to make certain their man won.

I couldn’t outspend the Sheriff, so I outworked him instead. I knocked on 15,000 doors, going through three pairs of shoes and two prosthetic legs. Against all odds, I WON THAT ELECTION!

Since then, I’ve been fighting for the people on the Upper Peninsula.  Jocelyn Benson tried to legalize ballot-harvesting, I sued her and WON. She tried accepting ballots that arrived ten days after the election, I sued her and WON. When she violated the 2nd Amendment to suppress the vote, I sued her and WON. I  fought the Governor, the Attorney General, the lobbyists, the media, and other legislators time and time again. I never stop fighting until I win.

This election, the odds are stacked against us. I'm going to beat the odds again. I'm going to fight like I've been doing my entire life.

FIGHT FOR ME on April 23rd, and together WE WILL WIN IN NOVEMBER!

{'Subject': 'Protect vulnerable citizens.', 'From': 'Kim Crockett <Kim@kimsos.com>', 'Message': [<p>Let's honor them. 
 ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

 

 

Kevin,

Elderly and homeless people are being exploited for their votes. Why do
election rules allow and encourage this?

When I was in high school, I worked as a nurse's aid in a residential
facility. I loved my patients! I helped them eat, bathe and get ready
for the day, or into bed at night. If walking was still an option,
we'd walk together in the hallway or even take a short stroll outside.
Some of the residents were sharp mentally but many suffered from some
loss of identity and memory.

There were quite a few characters who cracked me up with stories, songs
and even mischief when they got tired of the nurses' rules!

For your loved ones in nursing homes, take responsibility for protecting
them from those who might take advantage of their vulnerability. Make
sure no one else is ordering ballots for them, "helping" them vote, or
taking their ballots and voting for them. 

**Put written orders in their care instructions and speak to the
facility.**Please note: 

**designated agents MUST have a preexisting relationship with the
resident**. Unknown election "officials" or "election judges"
may not be designated agents if they don't have a prior relationship
with the resident.

**What about the homeless?** I have a good buddy who has worked as an
election judge in Minneapolis; he witnessed outright fraud in 2020.
Women were driving around in a golf cart picking up homeless people,
giving people a bag of candy (bribery under state statute) and then
helping them get registered to vote. The homeless just need to provide
an intersection in the precinct to qualify or same-day registration.
This went on all day long. 

There are "agent delivery" rules of ballots for nursing home
residents

on the SoS website as well as rules for the homeless to register and
vote
.

Give your family members' facility a link to Minnesota laws on
elections for Hospital Residents and Residents of Healthcare Facilities
so they follow the
law and aren't susceptible to those who might exploit it. But be
assertive when you know your loved one should not be voting.

https://kimsos.lt.acemlnb.com/Prod/link-tracker?redirectUrl=aHR0cHMlM0ElMkYlMkZ3d3cucmV2aXNvci5tbi5nb3YlMkZzdGF0dXRlcyUyRmNpdGUlMkYyMDNCLjEx&amp;sig=F98JFfxcH4nw9tikoBn4hhd42hmVJDJQbnekwjjzaroq&amp;iat=1649851732&amp;a=%7C%7C1001906488%7C%7C&amp;account=kimsos%2Eactivehosted%2Ecom&amp;email=O8xjJYmaqXcr9UfIRkvwzWQOP8ZXmRzMvz3Yw%2BcA7gI%3D&amp;s=7bb3c598e3065ac4a64753962f2c13b7&amp;i=55A60A1A390 

As Secretary of State, I would ask the Legislature to tighten the rules
around vulnerable populations like nursing homes residents, the homeless
and non-English speaking citizens. I would also monitor voting turnout
in nursing homes, for example, as a check on exploitation and fraud.

Just as importantly, I would ask the Legislature for extra stiff
penalties for the fraudsters who take advantage of the most vulnerable
among us, and then pursue prosecutions to punish and deter this kind of
abhorrent behavior.

Let's remember, you do not have to wait for tough, new legislation;
you can be on the lookout and advocate for your loved ones this election
cycle.

May you have a Blessed Easter weekend!

{'Subject': 'A Challenge and Invitation: Keeping the Holy in Holy Week', 'From': 'Kim Crockett <Kim@kimsos.com>', 'Message': [<p>Keep Holy Week Holy 
 ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

 

 

Kevin,

People of Faith always face the challenge of serving God while living in
a fallen world, dealing with practical demands and happy
responsibilities such as children and work. 

As a statewide candidate and a Christian, the challenge is great as I
enter Holy Week. The demands of the campaign are disrupting the time I
had set aside as the Lenten Season ends and I look forward to the
holiest week of the year and Easter Morning. 

As I talk with friends who are celebrating Passover and Ramadan, I note
with affection that this challenge is not unique to me.

And so let us unite around the prayer that people who love America and
want to live in Peace are filled with wisdom and strength as we face the
challenges of the day. The challenges are great. The cultural Marxists
and their opportunistic friends in the corporate media want to divide us
rather than help us find common ground so we can unite as We the People
and live in peace and prosperity. 

Our modern, high-tech culture is busy, noisy and threatens to overwhelm
us, especially conservatives who are under attack as the we work to
restore the promise of our Constitutional Republic and the right to live
in freedom as a self-governing people. 

Let's join hands, be thoughtful and kind to one another but also very
brave and strategic as we call out our mutual enemies who are working
day and night to bring America to her knees. 

I believe Minnesota is ground-zero in the culture and political wars.
This is a challenge and opportunity for all of us to lead our nation
back from the brink. Let's embrace the challenge with joy so we are
filled with strength, rather than exhausted by the challenges we face. 

Join me by putting God first; we can practice that commitment together,
no matter our faith tradition. 

May God Bless You and our Nation, 

Kim Crockett

Republican Candidate for Secretary of State
